Moore according to The Plant List (http://www.theplantlist.org/tpl1.1/record/tro-26603378) and Tropicos (https://www.tropicos.org/Name/26603378). Therefore, the accepted scientific name for this specimen should be Cheilanthes feei T. Moore.

Verification of the accepted scientific name from a source through a web search:
A search on GBIF (Global Biodiversity Information Facility; gbif.org) does not return an entry specifically for "Pleurozia chlorophylla"; instead it provides information for Pleurozia as a genus within the family Pleuroziaceae. Meanwhile, Tropicos (tropicos.org), another authoritative taxonomic database, lists Pleurozia chlorophyllium Lindb. as synonymous with Pleurozia subtilis (Hedw.) L. Söderstr., DeJean & A.M. Váňa. Considering the principles of priority and widespread usage in nomenclature, updating the accepted scientific name requires careful examination of latest taxonomic treatments by specialists. The verification process should check the most recent and accepted taxonomy reference specific to the organism, and make any corrections needed to the accepted scientific name accordingly.

My research is indicative and should be verified by checking the latest taxonomic databases or literature for the most current and accepted name for this specimen.
